supplier shall constitute a waiver of claims by that payee except those previously made in 
writing and identified by that payee as unsettled at the time of final Application for 
Payment. 
 
ARTICLE 10   PROTECTION OF PERSONS AND PROPERTY 
§ 10.1 SAFETY PRECAUTIONS AND PROGRAMS 
§ 10.1.1 The Contractor shall be responsible for initiating, maintaining and supervising 
all safety precautions and programs in connection with the performance of the Contract. 
 
§ 10.2 SAFETY OF PERSONS AND PROPERTY 
§ 10.2.1 The Contractor shall take reasonable precautions for safety of, and shall provide 
reasonable protection to prevent damage, injury or loss to: 
.1 employees on the Work and other persons who may be affected thereby; 
.2     visitors to the Project site;  
.3 the Work and materials and equipment to be incorporated therein, whether in 
storage on or off the site, under care, custody or control of the Contractor or 
the Contractor's Subcontractors or Sub-subcontractors; and 
.4 other property at the site or adjacent thereto, such as trees, shrubs, lawns, 
walks, pavements, roadways, structures and utilities not designated for 
removal, relocation or replacement in the course of construction. 
 
§ 10.2.2 The Contractor shall give notices and comply with applicable laws, ordinances, 
rules, regulations and lawful orders of public authorities bearing on safety of persons or 
property or their protection from damage, injury or loss. 
 
§ 10.2.3 The Contractor shall erect and maintain, as required by existing conditions and 
performance of the Contract, reasonable safeguards for safety and protection, including 
posting danger signs and other warnings against hazards, promulgating safety regulations 
and notifying owners and users of adjacent sites and utilities.  The Contractor shall also 
be responsible for all reasonable measures necessary to protect any property adjacent to 


===== PAGE 70 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
the Project and improvements thereon.  Any damage to such property or improvements 
shall be promptly repaired by the Contractor. 
 
§ 10.2.4 When use or storage of explosives or other hazardous materials or equipment or 
unusual methods are necessary for execution of the Work, the Contractor shall exercise 
utmost care and carry on such activities under supervision of properly qualified 
personnel. 
 
§ 10.2.5 The Contractor shall promptly remedy damage and loss (other than damage or 
loss insured under property insurance required by the Contract Documents) to property 
referred to in §§ 10.2.1.2 and 10.2.1.3 caused in whole or in part by the Contractor, a 
Subcontractor, a Sub-subcontractor, or anyone directly or indirectly employed by any of 
them, or by anyone for whose acts they may be liable and for which the Contractor is 
responsible under §§ 10.2.1.2 and 10.2.1.3, except damage or loss attributable to acts or 
omissions of the Owner or Architect or anyone directly or indirectly employed by either 
of them, or by anyone for whose acts either of them may be liable, and not attributable to 
the fault or negligence of the Contractor. The foregoing obligations of the Contractor are 
in addition to the Contractor's obligations under § 3.18. 
 
§ 10.2.6 The Contractor shall designate a responsible member of the Contractor's 
organization at the site whose duty shall be the prevention of accidents. This person shall 
be the Contractor's superintendent unless otherwise designated by the Contractor in 
writing to the Owner and Architect. 
 
§ 10.2.7 The Contractor shall not load or permit any part of the construction or site to be 
loaded so as to endanger its safety. 
 
§ 10.2.8 During the progress of the Work and at all times prior to the date of Substantial 
Completion or occupancy of the Work by the Owner, whichever is earlier, the Contractor 
shall provide temporary heat, ventilation, and enclosure, adequate to prevent damage to 
completed Work or Work in progress, or to materials stored on the premises. The 
permanent heating and ventilation systems may be used for these purposes (but at the 
Contractor’s sole cost and expense) when available unless otherwise provided in the 
Contract Documents. 
 
§ 10.2.9  The Contractor shall provide and maintain in good operating condition suitable 
and adequate fire protection equipment and services, and shall comply with all reasonable 
recommendations regarding fire protection made by the representatives of the fire 
insurance company carrying insurance on the Work or by the local fire chief for fire 
marshal. The area within the site limits shall be kept orderly and clean, and all 
combustible rubbish shall be promptly removed from the site. 
 
§ 10.2.10 The Contractor shall at all times protect the site, excavations, trenches, 
buildings and materials from rainwater, groundwater, backup or leakage of sewers, drains 
and other piping, and from water due to the Contractor’s and/or Subcontractor’s 
negligence and shall remove promptly the accumulation of water. Contractor shall 


===== PAGE 71 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
provide and operate all pumps, piping and other equipment necessary to this end at his 
sole risk and expense provided such is required because of Contractor’s Work or due to 
the Contractor’s negligent acts or omissions. The Contractor shall also keep the site free 
of accumulation of snow and ice. 
 
§ 10.2.11  Contractor shall take precautions necessary to prevent loss or damage caused 
by vandalism, theft, burglary, pilferage, or unexplained disappearance of property of the 
Owner located within the Project area, whether or not forming part of the Work.  
Contractor shall have full responsibility for the security of such property of the Owner 
located in such areas and shall reimburse the Owner for any such loss, damage or injury, 
except as may be directly caused by agents or employees of the Owner.  
 
§ 10.3 HAZARDOUS MATERIALS 
§ 10.3.1 If reasonable precautions will be inadequate to prevent foreseeable bodily injury 
or death to persons resulting from a material or substance, including but not limited to 
asbestos or polychlorinated biphenyl (PCB), encountered on the site by the Contractor, 
the Contractor shall, upon recognizing the condition, immediately stop Work in the 
affected area and report the condition to the Owner and Architect in writing. The 
Contractor shall have no responsibility for the discovery, presence, handling, removal, 
disposal or exposure of persons to hazardous substances existing in any form at the site 
unless the Contractor or anyone for whom Contractor is liable introduces the hazardous 
substance to the site, or unless the Contract Documents require the abatement and 
removal of said hazardous substances. 
 
§ 10.3.2 The Owner shall obtain the services of a licensed laboratory to verify the 
presence or absence of the material or substance reported by the Contractor and, in the 
event such material or substance is found to be present, to verify that it has been rendered 
harmless. Unless otherwise required by the Contract Documents, the Owner shall furnish 
in writing to the Contractor and Architect the names and qualifications of persons or 
entities who are to perform tests verifying the presence or absence of such material or 
substance or who are to perform the task of removal or safe containment of such material 
or substance. The Contractor and the Architect will promptly reply to the Owner in 
writing stating whether or not either has reasonable objection to the persons or entities 
proposed by the Owner. If either the Contractor or Architect has an objection to a person 
or entity proposed by the Owner, the Owner shall propose another to whom the 
Contractor and the Architect have no reasonable objection. When the material or 
substance has been rendered harmless, Work in the affected area shall resume upon 
written agreement of the Owner and Contractor, on which litigation has not been 
commenced, or by a court decision. The Contract Time shall be extended as appropriate, 
and the Contract Sum shall be increased in the amount of the Contractor's reasonable 
additional costs of shut-down and start-up, which adjustments shall be accomplished as 
provided in Article 7. Any such adjustments made to the Contract Sum in the Owner’s 
discretion shall be construed so as not to conflict with the “No Damages for Delay” 
provision in the Contract. 
 


===== PAGE 72 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
§ 10.3.3 To the fullest extent permitted by law, the Owner shall indemnify and hold 
harmless the Contractor, and its Subcontractors and employees from and against claims, 
damages, losses and expenses, including but not limited to attorneys' fees, arising out of 
or resulting from performance of the Work in the affected area if in fact the material or 
substance presents the risk of bodily injury or death as described in § 10.3.1 and has not 
been rendered harmless, provided that such claim, damage, loss or expense is attributable 
to bodily injury, sickness, disease or death, or to injury to or destruction of tangible 
property (other than the Work itself) and provided that such damage, loss or expense is 
not due to the sole negligence of a party seeking indemnity. 
 
§ 10.4 The Owner shall not be responsible under § 10.3 for materials and substances 
brought to the site by the Contractor unless such materials or substances were required by 
the Contract Documents and were obtained, handled and delivered in accordance with the 
Contract Documents. 
 
§ 10.5 EMERGENCIES 
§ 10.5.1 In an emergency affecting safety of persons or property, the Contractor shall act, 
at the Contractor's discretion, to prevent threatened damage, injury or loss. Additional 
compensation or extension of time claimed by the Contractor on account of an 
emergency shall be determined as provided in § 4.3 and Article 7. 
 
ARTICLE 11    INSURANCE AND BONDS  
THIS ARTICLE NOT USED.  SEE EXHIBIT J TO THE AGREEMENT 
ARTICLE 12   UNCOVERING AND CORRECTION OF WORK 
§ 12.1 UNCOVERING OF WORK 
§ 12.1.1 If a portion of the Work is covered contrary to the Architect's request or to 
requirements specifically expressed in the Contract Documents, it must, if required in 
writing by the Architect, be uncovered for the Architect's examination and be replaced at 
the Contractor's expense without change in the Contract Time. 
 
§ 12.1.2 If a portion of the Work has been covered which the Architect has not 
specifically requested to examine prior to its being covered, the Architect may request to 
see such Work and it shall be uncovered by the Contractor. If such Work is in accordance 
with the Contract Documents, costs of uncovering and replacement shall, by appropriate 
Change Order, be at the Owner's expense. If such Work is not in accordance with the 
Contract Documents, correction shall be at the Contractor's expense unless the condition 
was caused by the Owner or a separate contractor in which event the Owner shall be 
responsible for payment of such costs. 
 
§ 12.2 CORRECTION OF WORK 
§ 12.2.1 BEFORE OR AFTER SUBSTANTIAL COMPLETION 
§ 12.2.1.1 The Contractor shall promptly correct Work rejected by the Architect or failing 
to conform to the requirements of the Contract Documents, whether discovered before or 
after Substantial Completion and whether or not fabricated, installed or completed. Costs 
of correcting such rejected Work, including additional testing and inspections and 
compensation for the Architect's services and expenses made necessary thereby, shall be 


===== PAGE 73 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
at the Contractor's expense, including any cost, loss or damage to the Owner resulting 
from such failure or defect.  If prior to the date of Substantial Completion, the Contractor, 
a Subcontractor, or anyone for whom either is responsible uses or damages any portion of 
the Work, including, without limitation, mechanical, electrical, plumbing, and other 
building systems, machinery, equipment, or other mechanical device, the Contractor shall 
cause such item to be restored to “like new” condition at no expense to the Owner. 
 
§ 12.2.2 AFTER SUBSTANTIAL COMPLETION 
§ 12.2.2.1 In addition to the Contractor's obligations under § 3.5, if, within one year after 
the date of Final Completion of the Work or designated portion thereof, or after the date 
of completion of any corrective work, or after the date for commencement of warranties 
established under § 9.9.1, or by terms of an applicable special warranty required by the 
Contract Documents, whichever is later, any of the Work is found to be not in accordance 
with the requirements of the Contract Documents, the Contractor shall correct it promptly 
after receipt of written notice from the Owner to do so unless the Owner has previously 
given the Contractor an express written acceptance of such condition. The Owner shall 
give such notice to correct non-compliant Work promptly after discovery of the non-
compliant condition. During the applicable period for correction of Work, if the Owner 
fails to notify the Contractor and give the Contractor an opportunity to make the 
correction, the Owner waives the rights to require correction by the Contractor and to 
make a claim for breach of warranty. If the Contractor fails to correct nonconforming 
Work within a reasonable time during that period after receipt of notice from the Owner 
or Architect, the Owner may correct it in accordance with § 2.4. If any latent defect or 
deficiency arises or is discovered which was not active or apparent by reasonable 
inspection during the course of construction or before Substantial Completion is 
achieved, then the applicable period shall be extended by one (1) year after the discovery 
of the latent defect, subject to any applicable statute of repose. 
 
§ 12.2.2.2 The one (1) year period for correction of Work shall be extended with respect 
to portions of Work first performed after Substantial Completion by the period of time 
between Substantial Completion and the actual performance of the Work. 
 
§ 12.2.3 The Contractor shall remove from the site portions of the Work which are not in 
accordance with the requirements of the Contract Documents and are neither corrected by 
the Contractor nor accepted by the Owner. 
 
§ 12.2.4 The Contractor shall bear the cost of correcting destroyed or damaged 
construction, whether completed or partially completed, of the Owner or separate 
contractors caused by the Contractor's correction or removal of Work which is not in 
accordance with the requirements of the Contract Documents. 
 
§ 12.2.5 Nothing contained in this § 12.2 shall be construed to establish a period of 
limitation with respect to other obligations which the Contractor might have under the 
Contract Documents. Establishment of the one (1) year period for correction of Work as 
described in § 12.2.2 relates only to the specific obligation of the Contractor to correct 
the Work, and has no relationship to the time within which the obligation to comply with 


===== PAGE 74 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
the Contract Documents may be sought to be enforced, nor to the time within which 
proceedings may be commenced to establish the Contractor's liability with respect to the 
Contractor's obligations other than specifically to correct the Work. 
 
§ 12.3 ACCEPTANCE OF NONCONFORMING WORK 
§ 12.3.1 If the Owner prefers to accept Work which is not in accordance with the 
requirements of the Contract Documents, the Owner may do so instead of requiring its 
removal and correction, in which case the Contract Sum will be reduced as appropriate 
and equitable. Such adjustment shall be affected whether or not final payment has been 
made. 
 
ARTICLE 13   MISCELLANEOUS PROVISIONS 
 
§ 13.1 LAW AND CODES 
§ 13.1.1  The Contractor shall comply with all laws, codes, ordinances and regulations of 
the state, county, city, and/or municipality where the Project is located (New Jersey) and 
all applicable local jurisdictions therein) that pertain to performance of the Work.   
 
§ 13.2 SUCCESSORS AND ASSIGNS 
§ 13.2.1 Anti-Assignment Clause: The Contractor shall not assign the Contract without 
the prior, written consent of the Owner.  
 
§ 13.2.2 The Owner may, without consent of the Contractor, assign the Contract to any 
party it deems appropriate. The Contractor shall execute all consents reasonably required 
to facilitate such assignment(s). 
 
§ 13.3 WRITTEN NOTICE 
§ 13.3.1 Written notice shall be deemed to have been duly served if delivered in person to 
the individual or a member of the firm or entity or to an officer of the corporation for 
which it was intended, or if delivered at or sent by registered or certified mail to the last 
business address known to the party giving notice. 
 
§ 13.4 RIGHTS AND REMEDIES 
§ 13.4.1 Duties and obligations imposed by the Contract Documents and rights and 
remedies available thereunder shall be in addition to and not a limitation of duties, 
obligations, rights and remedies otherwise imposed or available by law. 
 
§ 13.4.2 No action or failure to act by the Owner, Architect or Contractor shall constitute 
a waiver of a right or duty afforded them under the Contract, nor shall such action or 
failure to act constitute approval of or acquiescence in a breach hereunder, except as may 
be specifically agreed in writing. 
 
§ 13.4.3 No consent or waiver, express or implied, by the Owner or the Architect to, or 
of, any breach of any covenant, condition or duty of the Contractor shall be construed as 
a consent to or waiver of any other breach of the same or any other covenant, condition or 
duty. Similarly, no consent or waiver, express or implied, by the Contractor to, or of, any 


===== PAGE 75 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
breach of any covenant, condition or duty of the Owner or the Architect shall be 
construed as a consent to or waiver of any other breach of the same or any other 
covenant, condition and/or duty. 
 
§ 13.5 TESTS AND INSPECTIONS 
§ 13.5.1 Tests, inspections and approvals of portions of the Work required by the 
Contract Documents or by laws, ordinances, rules, regulations or orders of public 
authorities having jurisdiction or by the requirements of any construction lender, 
permanent lender or other party with whom the Owner has a relationship (provided that 
such requirement have been disclosed to the Contractor) shall be made at an appropriate 
time. Unless otherwise provided, the Contractor shall make arrangements for, and shall 
schedule and coordinate, all such tests, inspections and approvals with an independent 
testing laboratory or entity acceptable to the Owner, or with the appropriate public 
authority, and shall bear all related costs of tests, inspections and approvals.  The 
Contractor shall give the Architect timely notice of when and where tests and inspections 
are to be made so that the Architect may be present for such procedures. The Owner shall 
bear costs of tests, inspections or approvals which do not become requirements prior to 
the effective date of this Agreement.  The Contractor shall bear all responsibility for 
expressly notifying the Owner and the Architect of any adverse testing or inspection 
results or reports that indicate lack of compliance with the Contract Documents, by 
indicating such lack of compliance clearly and expressly in such communications to the 
Owner and the Architect; mere transmission of testing and inspection reports to the 
Owner or the Architect without such express notification does not satisfy this contractual 
requirement.  Any tests or inspections performed by the Owner are for the Owner’s 
benefit only, and the results of any such tests shall not relieve the Contractor from strictly 
complying with the Contract Documents. 
 
§ 13.5.2 If the Architect, Owner or public authorities having jurisdiction determine that 
portions of the Work require additional testing, inspection or approval not included under 
§ 13.5.1, the Architect will, upon written authorization from the Owner, instruct the 
Contractor to make arrangements for such additional testing, inspection or approval by an 
entity acceptable to the Owner, and the Contractor shall give timely notice to the 
Architect of when and where tests and inspections are to be made so that the Architect 
may be present for such procedures. Such costs, except as provided in § 13.5.3, shall be 
at the Owner's expense. 
 
§ 13.5.3 If such procedures for testing, inspection or approval under §§ 13.5.1 and 13.5.2 
reveal failure of the portions of the Work to comply with requirements established by the 
Contract Documents, all costs made necessary by such failure including those of repeated 
procedures and compensation for the Architect's services and expenses shall be at the 
Contractor's expense. 
 
§ 13.5.4  The Contractor shall obtain and deliver promptly to the Owner any occupancy 
permit or any certificates of final inspection of any part of the Work or operating permits 
of any mechanical apparatus, such as elevators, escalators, boilers, air compressors, etc., 
which may be required by law to permit full use and occupancy of the premises by the 


===== PAGE 76 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
Owner. Receipt of such permits or certificates by the Owner shall be a condition 
precedent to Final Completion of the Work. All fees associated with obtaining the above 
shall be paid by the Contractor. 
 
§ 13.5.5 If the Architect is to observe tests, inspections or approvals required by the 
Contract Documents, the Architect will do so promptly and, where practicable, at the 
normal place of testing. 
 
§ 13.5.6 Tests or inspections conducted pursuant to the Contract Documents shall be 
made promptly to avoid unreasonable delay in the Work. 
 
§ 13.6 INTEREST 
§ 13.6.1 Payments due and unpaid under the Contract Documents shall bear interest from 
the date payment is due at such rate as the parties may agree upon in writing or, in the 
absence thereof, at the legal rate prevailing from time to time at the place where the 
Project is located. 
 
§ 13.7 GENERAL PROVISIONS 
 
§ 13.7.1 All personal pronouns used in this Contract, whether used in the masculine, 
feminine, or neuter gender, shall include all other genders; and the singular shall include 
the plural and vice versa. The titles of articles, paragraphs, subparagraphs and clauses are 
for convenience only, and neither limit nor amplify the provisions of this Contract in 
itself. 
 
§ 13.7.2 Any specific requirement in this Contract that the responsibilities or obligations 
of the Contractor also apply to a Subcontractor is added for emphasis and are also hereby 
deemed to include a Subcontractor of any tier. The omission of a reference to a 
Subcontractor in connection with any of the Contractor’s responsibilities or obligations 
shall not be construed to diminish, abrogate or limit any responsibilities or obligations of 
a Subcontractor of any tier under the Contract Documents or the applicable subcontract. 
 
§ 13.7.3  Any  statute of limitations with regard to a claim by the Owner against the 
Contractor may not commence to run and any alleged cause of action shall not be deemed 
to have accrued until the Owner has discovered the act or failure to act.  
 
ARTICLE 14   TERMINATION OR SUSPENSION OF THE CONTRACT 
§ 14.1 SUSPENSION OR TERMINATION BY THE CONTRACTOR 
 
§ 14.1.1 The Contractor may terminate the Contract upon seven (7) days’ written notice 
to the Owner if the Work has been stopped for a period of ninety (90) consecutive days 
through no act or fault of the Contractor or a Subcontractor, Sub-subcontractor or their 
agents or employees or any other persons or entities performing portions of the Work 
under direct or indirect contract with the Contractor, for any of the following reasons: 
 


===== PAGE 77 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
.1 issuance of an order of a court or other public authority having jurisdiction 
which requires all Work to be stopped; or  
 .2 an act of government, such as a declaration of national emergency which 
requires all Work to be stopped; or 
 .3 if the Work was stopped in accordance with Section 9.7.1. 
. 
§ 14.1.2 The Contractor may terminate the Contract if, through no act or fault of the 
Contractor or a Subcontractor, Sub-subcontractor or their agents or employees or any 
other persons or entities performing portions of the Work under direct or indirect contract 
with the Contractor, repeated suspensions, delays or interruptions of the entire Work by 
the Owner as described in § 14.3 constitute in the aggregate more than one hundred 
percent (100%) of the total number of days scheduled for completion, or ninety (90) days 
in any three hundred sixty-five (365)-day period, whichever is less. 
 
§ 14.1.3 If the Contract is terminated by Contractor under § 14.1.1 or 14.1.2, the 
Contractor shall only recover from the Owner such amount that would be recoverable 
from the Owner in the event of the Owner's termination for convenience under § 14.4 
below. 
 
§ 14.1.4  Notwithstanding any provision here, Contractor shall not stop performance in 
the event there is a bona fide dispute with the Owner regarding any of the reasons set 
forth in § 14.1.1 or 14.1.2.  The performance of the Work shall proceed without delay, 
but subject to Contractor’s right to assert a claim in accordance herewith.  
 
§ 14.2 TERMINATION BY THE OWNER FOR CAUSE  
§ 14.2.1 If the Contractor is adjudged a bankrupt, or if he makes a general assignment for 
the benefit of his creditors or if a receiver is appointed on account of his insolvency, or he 
persistently or repeatedly refuses or fails, except in cases of which extension of time is 
provided, to supply enough properly skilled workmen or proper materials, or if he fails to 
make payment to Subcontractors or for materials or labor as required by the terms of any 
agreement between Contractor and Subcontractor, or persistently disregards laws, 
ordinances, rules, regulations or orders of any public authority having jurisdiction, or if 
he repeatedly fails to meet the Contract  Schedule, or if he otherwise is guilty of a 
substantial violation of a provision of the Contract Documents, then the Owner may, 
without prejudice to any right or remedy and after giving the Contractor and his surety, if 
any, seven (7) days’ written notice, terminate the employment of the Contractor with 
respect to the entire Work or any portion thereof designated by the Owner and take 
possession of the site and of all materials, equipment, tools, construction equipment and 
machinery thereon owned by the Contractor and may finish the Work by whatever 
method he may deem expedient. The Contractor shall not be entitled to receive further 
payment until the Work is finished.  If the Contractor’s employment is terminated with 
respect to a portion of the Work only, he shall continue to perform the balance of the 
Work, but the Owner may withhold from the first sums payable to the Contractor in 
respect thereof an amount reasonable to fully protect Owner from loss.  The withheld 
amount, less any sums that the Owner is entitled to retain under Subparagraph 14.2.2, 
shall be paid to the Contractor when the terminated portion of the Work is completed.   


===== PAGE 78 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
 
§ 14.2.2 In the event of a complete or partial termination, the Contract Sum for the 
portion of the Work affected shall be reduced by the cost of finishing such portion of the 
Work, including compensation for the Architect’s services made necessary thereby and 
any overhead and all other direct costs incurred by the Owner, including, without 
limitation, all reasonable attorney’s fees, additional title costs, insurance, and additional 
interest because of any delay in completing the Work. If the reduction exceeds the unpaid 
balance of such Contract Sum, the Contractor shall pay the difference to the Owner. The 
Owner may at his option withhold and retain the difference from any other sums payable 
to the Contractor in respect of any portion of the Work. If such unpaid balance exceeds 
the reduction, the excess shall be applied as provided in the Agreement. The cost incurred 
by the Owner shall be certified by the Architect, upon application, in the manner 
provided in paragraph 9.4, and this obligation for payment shall survive the termination 
of the Contract. 
 
§ 14.2.3 If the Contractor disputes a termination of its right to perform with respect to a 
portion of the Work and the Owner’s withholding of funds as provided herein, then 
regardless of whether the Owner’s actions are subsequently determined to be wrongful, 
the Contractor shall nevertheless continue to perform the balance of the Work until a final 
determination is made, whereupon the Owner shall pay to the Contractor any additional 
sums to which the Contractor is determined to be entitled. 
 
§ 14.3 SUSPENSION BY THE OWNER FOR CONVENIENCE 
§ 14.3.1 The Owner may, without cause, order the Contractor in writing to suspend or 
interrupt the Work in whole or in part for such period(s) of time as the Owner may 
determine. 
 
§ 14.3.2 The Contract Sum and Contract Time shall be adjusted for increases in the cost 
and time caused by suspension or interruption as described in § 14.3.1. To the extent the 
Contractor has any additional costs attributable to the suspension or interruption as 
described in Subparagraph 14.3.1, the Contractor shall give the Owner written notice of 
such costs as soon as practicable after receiving notice of the suspension or interruption.  
Adjustment of the Contract Sum shall not include profit and shall only include site 
specific costs that affect the critical path of the Work.  Adjustment of the Contract Sum 
shall not include home office charges. No adjustment shall be made to the extent: 
.1 that performance is, was or would have been so suspended or interrupted by 
another cause for which the Contractor is responsible; or 
.2 that an equitable adjustment is made or denied under another provision of the 
Contract. 
This provision shall be construed in conjunction with the “No Damages for Delay” 
provision, and the Contractor agrees that this provision shall not be deemed to conflict 
with or create an ambiguity with such provision.  
 
§ 14.4 TERMINATION BY THE OWNER FOR CONVENIENCE 
§ 14.4.1 Notwithstanding the provisions contained in Article 14 herein, the Owner may 
terminate this Contract for its own convenience and without cause for any reason 


===== PAGE 79 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
whatsoever at any time, even though the Contractor is not in violation of a provision 
under the Contract Documents. If the Owner elects to terminate this Contract for its own 
convenience, the Owner shall notify the Contractor that the Owner has terminated the 
Work under the Contract and shall set the effective date of such termination. Upon 
receipt of any notice of such termination, the Contractor shall (a) immediately cancel all 
existing orders and subcontracts, (b) take all necessary measures for the protection and 
preservation of the property and Work performed hereunder, (c) immediately deliver to 
the Owner all plans, drawings, specifications and other information that was necessary 
for the performance of the Work, and (d) take all necessary actions to prevent further 
costs from being incurred by any person and/or entity performing work or supplying 
materials pursuant to the Contract Documents subsequent to the effective date of 
termination. 
 
§ 14.4.2 In the event the Owner terminates this Contract or a portion thereof pursuant to § 
14.4.1 above, the Owner shall reimburse the Contractor for all actual expenditures and 
costs incurred by the Contractor in the performance of its Work pursuant to the Contract 
Documents up through the date of termination (plus reasonable costs to terminate and 
demobilize as described below), subject to the limitations provided below. 
 
§ 14.4.2.1 The Contractor shall only be entitled to reimbursement for direct expenditures 
and reasonable costs incurred as a result of termination, and for Work actually performed. 
The Contractor shall not be entitled to be reimbursed for any indirect costs or fee for 
work not performed such as home office overhead, indirect field office overhead, interest, 
and settlement costs including, but not limited to, accounting fees. In a case where the 
Contractor intends to incur legal expenses to negotiate or contest a Subcontractor’s and/or 
vendor’s claim, the Contractor will obtain prior written approval from the Owner, which 
approval shall not be unreasonably withheld, to expend funds on legal costs. Legal and/or 
consulting fees shall be limited to reasonable amounts and those approved in writing by 
the Owner. 
 
§ 14.4.2.2 The Contractor shall only be entitled to reimbursement for direct expenditures 
and costs which were incurred prior to the effective date of termination, plus reasonable 
actual demobilization costs. 
 
§ 14.4.2.3 The Contractor shall only be entitled to reimbursement for direct expenditures 
and costs which were reasonably incurred and approved by the Owner. 
 
§ 14.4.3 The amount, if any, to be paid to the Contractor shall not cause the Guaranteed 
Maximum Price to be exceeded, nor shall it exceed an amount calculated as follows: 
 
 § 14.4.3.1 Take the Cost of the Work incurred plus reasonable costs to terminate 
and demobilize as described above by the Contractor to the date of termination; 
 
§ 14.4.3.2 Add the Contractor's Fee computed upon the Cost of the Work to the 
date of termination; and 
 


===== PAGE 80 =====
 
Initials ___/___ 
 
 § 14.4.3.3 Subtract the aggregate of previous payments made by the Owner. 
 
The Owner shall also be credited for: (i) payments previously made to the Contractor for 
the terminated portion of the Work, (ii) claims which the Owner has against the 
Contractor under the Contract and (iii) the sums recovered as fair market value of the 
materials, supplies, equipment or other items that are to be disposed of by the Contractor 
that are part of the Contract Sum.  Contractor shall not be entitled to receive profit and 
overhead on the Work not executed. 
 
§ 14.4.4   Deleted 
 
§ 14.4.5   All obligations of the Contractor under the Contract Documents with respect to 
completed Work shall remain in full force and effect. 
 
§ 14.4.6   Any termination by the Owner or payments made to the Contractor shall be 
without prejudice to any claim or legal remedies which the Owner may have against the 
Contractor for any cause pursuant to the Contract Documents. 
 
§ 14.4.7   All subcontracts and/or purchase orders entered into by the Contractor shall 
include a similar termination for convenience clause.

GENERAL 
1. Proposal based on a merit shop project. 
2. Building Permit Fees are to be by Owner.  Trade Permit Fees included as a Not to Exceed Allowance. 
3. Builder’s Risk is included as an allowance. 
4. Gross receipts taxes and, business privilege taxes are not included 
5. Testing and inspections to be provided by the Owner.  IMC specifically includes coordination with 3rd 
party special inspectors for timely site visits to maintain project schedule.  
6. Except as specifically required to be Contractor design responsibility, Owner to provide all design 
and engineering services including Architectural, Structural, MEP, and Civil drawings adequate for 
construction permits.  All designs are assumed to be code compliant and comply with all fire 
ratings.  All design to be coordinated between all consultants. 
7. ALTA survey is excluded. 
8. Subcontractor Default Insurance is included within trades. 
9. We have assumed Contractor can present an “or equal” “non-proprietary” product for all products 
subject to reasonable approval by Architect at time of submittal.  All products included in 
manufacturer’s standard colors and finishes unless otherwise specified in Contract Documents.  The 
‘‘or equal” “non-proprietary” items, when submitted, shall include the cost and lead time variance, if 
applicable, as part of the substitution approval process.  These substitutions are subject to approval 
by Owner, which will not be unreasonably withheld.  
10. Subcontractor Insurance is included in schedule of values. 
11. Owner FF&E is excluded except for where Contract Documents specifically call for Contractor to 
provide (labor and/or installation). 
12. Dumpsters for Owners FF&E are excluded.  
13. Temporary site perimeter fencing is included.  Site security guard during normal or off-hours, sensors, 
cameras, police used for means of security, and off-hours labor or supervision for security purposes 
are excluded. 
14. Temporary utility consumption fees are included as an Owner Directed Allowance. 
15. Winter and temporary weather conditions such as temporary heating, cooling, 
dehumidification, snow / ice / rain removal, temporary partitions / plastic etc., winter additives 
and surcharges and associated provisions are included as an allowance. 
16. Insurance is based on IMC CCIP Insurance Program. 
17.  This budget reflects current market prices as of February 7, 2023 and does not allow for 
unusual price escalations.  Provided Contractor expeditiously locks in all subcontractor and 
vendor pricing upon receipt of the Notice to Proceed, the GMP shall be equitably adjusted 
for any extreme market driven price changes beyond Contractor’s control, defined as an 
industrywide price increase by suppliers after February 7, 2023 that can be documented, 
substantiated, and is otherwise unavoidable.  Contractor is not aware of any industrywide 
price increase between February 7, 2023 and May 31, 2023 affecting GMP.  Based on a 
Limited NTP dated March 3, 2023 and June 2, 2023, , IMC has issued LOI’s to the below

PROJECT SPECIFIC REFLECTED CEILING PLAN NOTES: 
1. SEE SHEETS A5.01 THROUGH A5.12 FOR RESIDENT ROOM  TYPICAL CEILING PLANS. 
2. ALL GWB CEILINGS AND SOFFITS TO BE PAINTED CEILI NG WHITE UNLESS NOTED 
OTHERWISE. 
3. REFER TO A5.30 FOR MOULDING PROFILES. 
4. ELECTRICIAN IS TO REVIEW MILLWORK DRAWINGS FOR A NY LIGHTING FIXTURES 
LOCATED IN MILLWORK. 
5. CHANDELIER LIFT TO BE INSTALLED BY CONTRACTOR, I NSTALLED REMOTELY LOCATED 
MECHANIZED LIFT ABOVE FINISHED CEILINGS FOR CHANDEL IER, MODIFY ABOVE CEILING 
STRUCTURE AS REQUIRED.  ALADDIN LIGHT LIFT #ALL200R M-CM INSTALLED PER 
MANUFACTURERS INSTRUCTIONS.  SEE A6.02A FOR LOCATIO N. REP INFO: ZACHARY 
BARRY 256.429.9700 
6. BIDDING CONTRACTORS TO INCLUDE UNIT PRICING FOR ALL LIGHTING FIXTURE 
SPECIFICATIONS ON ELECTRICAL ENGINEER DWGS. 
7. IN LOCATIONS WHERE ACCENT MATERIAL IS CALLED OUT  IN A TRAY CEILING, ONLY THE 
HORIZONTAL SURFACE IS TO RECEIVE THAT MATERIAL AND SURROUNDING VERTICAL 
SURFACES ARE TO BE CEILING WHITE, U.N.O. 
8. IN LOCATIONS WHERE ACCENT MATERIAL IS CALLED OUT  ON A SOFFIT, ALL EXPOSED 
EDGES OF SOFFIT ARE TO BE ACCENT MATERIAL.

Selections.

use of a MDF product or similar? Garden State Lumber MDF Products
VM#16 – Can IMC get us photos/site location where you have utilized the stone imprint fence
previously?
VM#17 – Can IMC clarify what is included in the $41k. I know this is a “Target” VM, but what got
you to this number?  This is a percentage reduction target given by a lighting supplier based of their
 analysis of the package. They feel this would be a realistic reduction based on reselection of certain
fixtures.
VM#18 – IMC to get itemized list from Clark showing how we achieve this savings See list below in
reference documents.

subcontractors they feel that this is an target cost percentage reduction if select design
modifications 
are made.

should be older than 5 years See photos below in reference documents.

so that they can be verified by Bala See marked up plan in below reference documents.
VM#26 – Can IMC send a mark-up of the elevation showing what is included as Vinyl Siding? See
marked up plan in below reference documents.

please provide a breakdown on this See below breakdown in reference doc
VM#29 – IMC to provide electric fireplace spec that gets us to this number. See below potential
specifications in below reference documents.
VM#35 – IMC to confirm if this includes colored concrete? Confirmed
VM#37 – Can IMC get a breakout from their drywall guy for what was carried for these column
wraps. $32,000 
VM#38 – Can IMC ask around to their plumbers for any previous experience with the rental
equipment, or any recommended companies that rent out this equipment.

EXHIBIT J 
 
INSURANCE REQUIREMENTS 
 
 
1. COVERAGE AND LIMITS TO BE PROVIDED BY CO NTRACTOR: Prior to the 
commencement of any of the Work, Contractor shall maintain, and require that all Subcontractors, 
Sub-subcontractors, and suppliers (of any tier), through the terms and provisions of any such Contracts 
or Subcontracts, maintain appropriate levels of insurance including the minimum coverages and limits 
identified herein for the duration of the Project and as required after completion. 
 
Owner reserves the right in its sole discretion to reject; withhold permission to enter the Project site 
and/or commence work; suspend work; or terminate for cause any Contractor, Subcontractor, or Sub-
subcontractor (of any tier) for failure to satisfy the insurance requirements herein or failure to comply 
with the provisions of the Contract Documents including the General Conditions and Exhibits. 
 
Contractor shall secure and keep in full force and effect, and shall cause its Subcontractors and Sub -
subcontractors (of every tier) to secure and keep in full force and effect, throughout the term of this 
Agreement, commencing with the earlier of commencement of work or access to the Project Site, and 
continuing through completion of performance of the work and for a specified period of time thereafter 
as provided in this Article, with terms and conditions as specified, the following coverages at the 
Contractor’s sole cost and expense: 
 
A. Commercial/Business Automobile Liability Insurance .  Such insurance shall be written on a 
current ISO form CA 00 01 and cover all owned, non-owned, and hired vehicles used in connection 
with the Work, and provide limits of at least $1,000,000 per accident for bodily injury and property 
damage.  The required limit may be met with any combination of primary and Excess/Umbrella 
coverage. 
i. Should any covered automobile be used to transport hazardous materials, the operator the 
automobile shall provide FMCSA Form MCS 90, and the applicable policy shall be 
endorsed with ISO form CA 99 48. 
ii. The policies must be further endorsed to: 
1) Name the Owner and the parties listed below  (individually, an “Owner 
Party” and collectively, the “Owner Parties”), as additional insureds; 
2) Stipulate that such insurance is primary and is not contributing with, any 
other insurance carried by, or for the benefit of the additional insureds; 
3) Waive any and all rights of subrogation against the Owner Parties; and 
4) Include, when required by the Motor Carrier Act of 1980, a MCS -90 
endorsement applicable to liability arising out of the transportation of hazardous 
materials or waste. 
B. Workers’ Compensation (including but not limited to coverage or endorsements for Occupational 
Disease Benefits, Voluntary Compensation and Disability benefits, Jones A ct and U.S. 
Longshoremen's and Harbor Worker's Act, if applicable) – Statutory Workers’ Compensation and 
Employer’s Liability with limits of no less than $1,000,000 each accident for bodily injury by 
accident; $1,000,000 policy limit for both bodily injury  by disease; and $1,000,000 each employee 
J-1

===== PAGE 164 =====
for bodily injury by disease.  Such policy must be further endorsed to  waive any and all rights of 
subrogation against the Owner Parties. 
 
C. Commercial General Liability Insurance .  Commercial General Liability insurance with the 
following limits of liability: 
 
Each Occurrence Limit:  $1,000,000.00 
Personal/Advertising Injury Aggregate:  $2,000,000.00 
Annual General Aggregate:  $2,000,000.00 
Products/Completed Operations Aggregate: $2,000,000.00 
 
This insurance shall be broad form and written on a current ISO CG 00 01 “Occurrence” Form and 
coverage shall apply to any and all claims arising out of bodily injury, property damage, premises 
and operations, products and comple ted operations, independent contractors, personal and 
advertising injury, and contractual liability. These limits should apply based upon a per project and/or 
per location basis, and the General Aggregate Limit shall reinstate annually.  Such policy(ies) m ust 
be further endorsed to:  
1) Include the Owner Parties as additional insureds for both ongoing and completed operations 
work. General liability coverage shall be endorsed using ISO additional insured forms CG 20 10 
07 04 and CG 20 37 07 04 or equivalent sp ecifically listing the Owner Parties as additional 
insureds.  
2) Stipulate that such insurance is primary and non -contributory and will not seek contribution 
from any other insurance carried by, or for the benefit of the additional insureds, including all 
applicable deductibles or retentions; 
3) Waive any and all rights of subrogation against all of the Owner Parties;  
4) Contain cross liability and severability of interest endorsements, and a separation of insureds 
provision acceptable to the Owner; 
5) Provide products and completed operations coverage, extending for a period of not less than the 
later to occur of (i) ten (10) years after final completion of the entire Work or (ii) the applicable 
statute of repose for the jurisdiction where the Work is located.  Additional insured status for the 
Owner Parties shall be provided during construction of the project through the Completed 
Operations Period of a period not less than the later to occur of (i) ten (10) years after the final 
completion of the entire Work or (ii) the applicable statute of repose for the jurisdiction where 
the Work is located; 
6) Provide personal injury coverage including, but not limited to, false arrest, detention or 
imprisonment or malicious prosecution; libel, slander or defam ation of character, invasion of 
privacy, wrongful eviction or wrongful entry, harassment of any kind and discrimination; 
7) Provide $1,000,000 broad form contractual liability per occurrence coverage; 
8) Provide coverage for residential construction operations. General liability policies containing 
exclusions for residential construction, or an exclusion for residential apartment construction, are 
not acceptable to project owner;   
J-2

===== PAGE 165 =====
9) Provide for hostile fire coverage and fire legal liability coverage; 
10) Provide for coverage for certified acts of domestic terrorism; 
11) Provide for minimum of $100,000 elevator collision coverage; and 
12) Provide for a deductible of no greater than $5,000 per claim unless higher amounts are 
approved by Owner in writing prior to commencement of Work. 
13) Contactor is required to notify the Owner Parties of any claim or claims that erode the available 
aggregate limit by fifty percent (50%) or more. Owner Parties reserve the ability to require 
contractor to purchase additional coverage limits to restore the available limit of insurance to the 
amounts required in this Exhibit and/or the Contract Documents. 
 
D. Excess and/or Umbrella Liability. Contractor, Subcontractors and Sub-subcontractors (of every 
tier) shall provide excess liability limits in the form of an umbrella or excess liability policy, with 
coverage at least as broad as the Commercial/Business Automobile Liability, Employers Liability, 
and Commercial General Liability insurance required herein.  Contractor may satisfy the limits of 
liability required herein with a combination of primary, umbrella, and/or excess policies of 
insurance where applicable, provided that such policies comply with all of the provisions herein.  
All such policies shall include a duty to defend additional insureds and shall state that the coverage 
afforded to the additional insureds is primary and non-contributory to any other insurance, 
including self-insurance, maintained by the additional insureds, whether such other insurance be 
primary, excess or on any other basis.  Such excess insurance shall be maintained for a period of not 
less than ten (10) years beyond Substantial Completion of the entire Project, or the applicable 
statute of repose for the jurisdiction where the Work is located, whichever is longer; 
 . 
i. Umbrella Excess Liability with limits of no less than $15,000,000 each occurrence and 
$15,000,000 aggregate providing following form excess over the General Liability, 
Automotive Liability and Employer’s Liability p olicies described above.  This insurance 
shall by its following form excess provisions or endorsement:  
1) Protect the Owner Parties as additional insureds for both ongoing and completed 
operations of Contractor; 
2) Stipulate that such insurance is primary to and is not contributing with any other 
insurance carried by, or for the benefit of the additional insureds; 
3) Waive any and all rights of subrogation against all Owner Parties; and 
4) Provide products and completed operations liability coverage, extending for a p eriod 
not less than the later to occur of (i) ten (10) years after final completion of the entire 
Work or (ii) the applicable statute of repose for the jurisdiction where the Work is 
located. Additional insured status for the Owner Parties shall be provide d during 
construction of the project and through the Completed Operations Period of a period 
not less than the later to occur of (i) ten (10) years after final completion of the entire 
Work or (ii) the applicable statute of repose for the jurisdiction wher e the Work is  
located. 
5) Contactor is required to notify the Owner Parties of any claim or claims that erode the 
available aggregate limit by fifty percent (50%) or more. Owner Parties reserve the 
J-3

===== PAGE 166 =====
ability to require contractor to purchase additional coverage limits to restore the 
available limit of insurance to the amounts required in this Exhibit and/or the Contract 
Documents. 
 
E. Specific Limitations and Requirements.   Contractor’s Commercial General Liability and 
Excess/Umbrella Liability insurance must comply with each of the following: 
1) Contain no limitation or exclusion for resulting or consequential loss arising from property 
damage. 
2) Contain no limitation or exclusion for loss due to explosion, collapse, or underground 
property. 
3) Contain no limitation or exclusion for liability arising out of mobile equipment. 
4) Contain no limitation or exclusion for an additional insured’s vicarious liability, strict liability, 
or statutory liability including, without limitation, liability pursuant to New York’s labor laws. 
5) Contain no limitation or exclusion based on the existence of project-specific Owner’s interest 
general liability policy. 
6) Contain no professional liability exclusion applicable to services generally considered part of 
means and methods for a particular trade (i.e. , no more restrictive than ISO Form 22 79 07 
98) 
7) Include full severability of interests for insureds (i.e., no exclusion for cross -liability or 
insured-versus-insured applicable to suits between the Contractor and Owner or  Owner's 
Indemnified Parties). 
8) Contain no height restriction(s). 
F. Professional Liability Insurance. Professional Liability Insurance for any and all claims for bodily 
injury, property damage, and/or financial damages as a result of wrongful acts arising out  of the 
performance or failure to perform professional services in the amount not less than the greater of 
$1,000,000 or ten percent (10%) of the construction contract amount each claim/aggregate. The 
definition of professional services must be appropriate to include all professional services performed 
by or on behalf of the Contractor for the Owner Parties and/or at the Project. 
i. If written on a claims -made policy form, the policy retroactive date is to be on or before 
the first date of professional service s provided by or on behalf of the Contractor for the 
Owner Parties and/or at the Project. 
ii. Contractor is required to maintain professional liability, when required, and shall cause all 
subcontractors that are providing Design Services to maintain profession al liability 
coverage for the duration of the project and maintain coverage (or purchase an extended 
reporting period if coverage is not renewed) for a period not less than the later to occur of 
(i) six (6) years after final completion of the entire Work o r (ii) the applicable statute of 
repose for the jurisdiction where the Work is located. 
iii. Contactor is required to notify the Owner Parties of any claim or claims that erode the 
available aggregate limit by fifty percent (50%) or more. Owner Parties reserve the ability 
J-4

===== PAGE 167 =====
to require contractor to purchase additional coverage limits to restore the available limit of 
insurance to the amounts required in this Exhibit and/or the Contract Documents.    
 
G. Contractor’s Property Insurance .  Contractor , and Sub-subcontractors (of any tier)  shall be 
responsible for insuring its own tools, equipment, and facilities, including owned or rented mobile 
equipment.   
i. Contractor and Subcontractors and Sub-subcontractors (of any tier) will be responsible for 
insuring their own tools and equipment on an “All Risk Basis” covering physical damage 
to all tools and equipment, including automotive equipment, with limits at least high 
enough to provide for replacement of items necessary to complete the Work, other than 
those specifically insured by the Builder’s Risk Insurance Policy maintained by the Owner. 
 
H. Pollution Liability Insurance for any and all claims for damages due to pollution incidents arising 
out of construction operations of the project in the amount of not less than $2,000,000 per 
occurrence/aggregate.  This insurance shall be maintained during the course of the construction of 
the Project and completed operations coverage for a period not less than the later to occur of (i) six 
(6) years after final completion of the entire Work or (ii) the applicable statute of repose for the 
jurisdiction where the Work is located.  Such policy must be further endorsed to: 
i. Name the Owner Parties as additional insureds for both the ongoing and completed 
operations of the Contractor; 
ii. Stipulate that such insurance is primary and is not contributing with, any other insurance 
carried by, or for the benefit of the additional insureds; 
iii. Waive any and all right of subrogation against all of the Owner Parties; 
iv. Provide coverage for mold, fungi, and bacteria related claims arising out of the construction 
of the project; and 
v. Coverage shall be written on an occurrence basis. If occurrence-based coverage forms are 
not available to the Contractor and coverage is written on a claims -made policy form, the 
policy retroactive date is to be on or before the first date of operations are performed by or 
on behalf of the Owner Parties.  Claims made coverage will include a six (6) year extended

Exhibit.  The limits of insurance stated  in this Exhibit are  minimum limits only.  In the event 
Contractor’s policy provides greater limits, then the additional insureds shall be entitled to, or to 
share in, the full limits of such policy, and this Exhibit shall be deemed to require such full limits.

to an additional insured shall be no broader than that req uired by contract, or words of similar 
meaning, the parties agree that nothing in this Agreement is intended to restrict or limit the breadth 
of such coverage.

excess of $10,000 unless authorized in writing in advance by the Owner.  Applicable deductibles 
of any policy required herein shall be the responsibility of the party procuring such coverage.

5. CONTRACTOR'S LIABILITY INSURANCE AND SUBCONTRACTOR DEFAULT

A. The Contractor shall procure and maintain in effect during the term of this Agreement through at

requirements and provisions herein.  
 
B. The Contractor shall obtain payment and performance bonds from individual Subcontractors for all 
subcontracts in excess of $250,000 or as otherwise required by Owner.  Alternatively, at the 
Owner’s option, the Contractor shall obtain and provide Subcontrac tor Default Insurance (“SDI”) 
to cover the performance of the Subcontractors, Sub -subcontractors and Suppliers in connection 
with the Project, in form and substance reasonably acceptable to the Owner.  The cost of all such 
bonds or SDI shall be included in  the GMP.  Contractor shall propose to Owner, in writing, the 
minimum limits for any such SDI policy coverage including proposed minimum limits of per claim 
and in the aggregate for the Project, which are subject to Owner’s written approval.  The SDI policy 
must include a “Financial Interest Endorsement” for the benefit of the Owner, the Additional 
Insureds and any Lenders.  The cost of the SDI (if applicable) shall be in place of Subcontractors’ 
payment and performance bonds.  If bonds are utilized, a premium invoice from the subcontractor’s 
agent shall be provided which shall evidence with particularity the amount chargeable as a Cost of 
Work for this Project per the Contract Documents and Exhibits thereto, which must be approv ed 
by Owner in writing.   
 
C. In no event shall Owner be charged for any such payment and performance bonds and the SDI for 
the same Subcontractor.  The Contractor shall provide the Owner with access to and an opportunity 
to review the Contractor’s complete S DI policy, including, without limitation, all policy 
endorsements and forms, declarations page(s), exclusions, indirect cost coverage, deductibles, co-
pay requirements, Subcontractor prequalification requirements and procedures and  any 
documentation provided by a Subcontractor in response to such prequalification procedures.   In 
addition, Contractor shall provide the Owner with a statement from the SDI carrier and/or broker 
evidencing any erosion of the per occurrence or aggregate limits  upon Contract execution and 
thereafter at three (3) month intervals , upon any material changes to the remaining limits of such 
policy, and at Owner’s request.

are necessary under the applicable Subcontract in connection with an event of default and (ii) make

diligently administer and pursue resolution of the claim.  If, after consultation between the Owner 
and the Contractor, the Owner requests that the General Contractor default a Subcontractor and the 
Contractor refuses to default such Subcontractor, the Contractor shall, at its sole cost and expense 
and without the use of the Contingency, be responsible for all costs, dam ages and delays arising 
from such Subcontractor’s default or failure to perform.  If after consultation between the Owner 
and Contractor, the Owner requests that the Contractor default a Subcontractor and the Contractor 
elects not to default such Subcontra ctor for default of performance, the Contingency may only be 
used if the Contractor demonstrates to Owner, in Owner’s reasonable discretion, that continued 
performance by the Subcontractor is in the best interests of the Project, including prosecution of 
the Work in accordance with the Project Schedule, relative to utilizing a replacement subcontractor 
and/or defaulting the subcontractor and allowing them to remain on the job while the claim is 
pending with the SDI carrier(s) , and Owner agrees to same in wr iting.  The General Contractor 
shall take such actions without regard to any applicable deductible under the SDI policy.

the Contract as of the date of such request and thereafter. 
6. Construction Manager agrees that Lender shall at all times have the right, but not the 
obligation, to enforce, at Owner’s sole cost and expense, the performance or observance of each and 
every covenant, obligation and condition of the Contract to be performed or observed by Construction 
Manager.  Furthermore, in the event of any default by Owner occurring and continuing under the Loan 
Agreement, as confirmed to Construction Manager by written notice from Lender, Construction 
Manager agrees that Lender may elect to succeed to and exercise all of Owner’s rights and privileges 
and to assume all of Owner’s obligations under the Contract accruing from and after such notice and 
that Construction Manager shall be absolutely protected against Owner in proceeding in reliance on 
such notice from Lender.

7. Construction Manager agrees that Lender  shall have no liability or obligations to 
Construction Manager either under the Contract, the General Collateral Assignment, or otherwise, for

obligations of Owner under the Contract, and then only with respect to obligations accruing from and 
after such assumption.  Notwithstanding the foregoing, Lender agrees that Construction Manager shall 
not be obligated to perform any servic es or complete construction of the work unless and until 
Construction Manager has received all sums then due, as of the date of the Lender’s election, under 
the terms of the Contract. 
8. Construction Manager agrees that during the course of construction and after receipt 
of notice of Owner’s default under the Loan Documents, Construction Manager shall deliver to Lender 
copies of such waivers and releases of liens by Construction Manager and received by Construction 
Manager by trade contractors engaged by Construction Manager, as provided for in the Contract.  Prior

notice of Owner’s default under the Loan Documents, Construction Manager shall deliver to Owner, 
with a copy to Lender, a complete release of liens (or copy thereof) signed by Construction Manager 
and all its direct subcontractors and materialmen, if any. 
9. Construction Manager agrees that it will use its reasonable commercial efforts to 
include in each subcontract hereafter executed between Construction Manager, acting as Lender  of 
Owner, and a subcontractor performing work to be performed in connection with the Project shall 
include a provision whereby the subcontractor agrees that: (a) such subcontractor agrees to execute 
and deliver to Construction Manager, Owner and Lender, prior to final payment, a complete release of 
liens; (b) if Construction Manager, acting as Lender of Owner, or Owner materially defaults under the 
subcontract, the subcontractor shall give written notice to Owner and Lender specifying the material 
default and the steps necessary to cure such default, and Owner and/or Lender  shall have the right to 
cure any material defaults by Construction Manager or Owner under such subcontract for a period of 
thirty (30) days after receipt of such notice (or such longer period after receipt of such notice as may 
be necessary to cure such default) during which period the subcontractor shall forbear exercising any 
remedy it may have with respect to such default, it being understood that Owner and Lender shall have 
no obligation to cure any such defaults, and (c) following a default by Construction Manager under the 
Contract, at the requ est of Owner and/or Lender , the subcontractor will continue performance under 
the subcontract in accordance with its terms so long as the subcontractor shall be paid in accordance 
with the subcontract for all work, labor and materials furnished pursuant thereto, and, to the extent 
such contract is not freely assignable by Owner, will enter into a new subcontract with a contractor to 
be approved by Owner and Lender upon substantially the same term s and conditions as the original 
subcontract.  Construction Manager further agrees to furnish Lender upon request with a copy of each 
fully executed subcontract. 
10. Any notices to be sent by Construction Manager hereunder to Lender shall be in writing 
and sent via registered or certified mail, return receipt requested, or by express courier service 
guarantying overnight delivery, in either case to the address set forth in the caption or to such other 
address as Lender may hereafter designate by appropriate written notice to Construction Manager. 
11. Nothing herein contained shall be construed to impose upon any of the Secured Parties 
any duty to advance funds to Owner except upon and subject to the terms of the Loan Agreement, or 
to see to the application of the proceeds of the Loan.  Construction Manager acknowledges that it has

EXHIBIT A 
ADDITIONAL DEFINED TERMS 
“Banking Services” means each and any of the following bank services provided to Borrower by the 
Lender or an Affiliate:  (a) commercial credit cards, (b) stored value cards and (c) treasury and/or cash 
management services (including controlled disbursement, automated clearinghouse transactions, 
return items, overdrafts and interstate depository network services). 
“Ba nking Services Obligations” means any and all obligations of Borrower, whether absolute or 
contingent and howsoever and whenever created, arising, evidenced or acquired (including all 
renewals, extensions and modifications thereof and substitutions therefor) in connection with Banking 
Services. 
“A
ffiliate ” means, with respect to a specified Person, another Person that directly, or indirectly through 
one or more intermediaries, Controls or is Controlled by or is under common Control with the Person 
specified, including, but not limited to, an entity in which such Person owns more than ten percent 
(10%) of the equity interests. 
“Cont rol ” means the possession, directly or indirectly, of the power to direct or cause the direction of 
the management or policies of a Person, whether through the ability to exercise voting power, by 
contract or otherwise.  “Controlling” and “Controlled” have meanings correlative thereto. 
“Hedging Contracts” means interest rate swap agreements, interest rate cap agreements and interest 
rate collar agreements, or any other agreements or arrangements entered into between the Borrower 
and any Lender (excepting interest rate cap agreements, which may be entered into with a Qualified 
Financial Institution) and designed to protect the Borrower against fluctuations in interest rates or 
currency exchange rates, in form and substance reasonably acceptable to Lender. 
“H
edging Obligations ” means, with respect to the Borrower, all liabilities of the Borrower to any 
Lender under Hedging Contracts. 
“Inde mnitee ” means Lender and each Lender, and each Related Party of Lender or any Lender. 
“Loan Documents” means the Loan Agreement, Promissory Note executed by Borrower in favor of 
Lender, the Mortgage and Security Agreement of even date with the Loan Agreement executed by 
Borrower in favor of Lender , as amended, modified, restated or replaced from time to time , the 
Assignment of Leases and Rents of even date with the Loan Agreement executed by Borrower in favor 
of Lender, as amended from time to time , any and all any Completion Guaranty Agreement s, in the 
form of required by the Loan Agreement in favor of Lender, as amended from time to time, that certain 
Environmental Indemnity Agreement of even date with the Loan Agreement  in favor of Lender, as 
amended from time to time , the Property Manager Subordination Agreement of even date with the 
Loan Agreement executed by property manager in favor of Lender, as amended from time to time, and 
any and all other documents now or hereafter executed by Borrower, CSH West Orange Lessee, LLC, 
any present or future, direct and indirect subsidiaries of Borrower, or any other guarantor of the 
Obligations or any portion thereof evidencing, guarantying, or securing or otherwise expressly stating 
it relates to the Obligations; provided, however, that Hedging Contracts between Borrower and Lender 
or Affiliate of Lender shall not constitute Loan Documents.
